         <img alt="{\begin{bmatrix}X_{B}\\Y_{B}\\Z_{B}\end{bmatrix}}={\begin{bmatrix}X_{A}\\Y_{A}\\Z_{A}\end{bmatrix}}+{\begin{bmatrix}\Delta X_{A}\\\Delta Y_{A}\\\Delta Z_{A}\end{bmatrix}}+{\begin{bmatrix}1&amp;-r_{z}&amp;r_{y}\\r_{z}&amp;1&amp;-r_{x}\\-r_{y}&amp;r_{x}&amp;1\end{bmatrix}}\cdot {\begin{bmatrix}X_{A}-X_{A}^{0}\\Y_{A}-Y_{A}^{0}\\Z_{A}-Z_{A}^{0}\end{bmatrix}}+\Delta S{\begin{bmatrix}X_{A}-X_{A}^{0}\\Y_{A}-Y_{A}^{0}\\Z_{A}-Z_{A}^{0}\end{bmatrix}}." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0526dfb426440b28df9710fc68036ed5b82ecb14" style="vertical-align: -4.671ex; width:88.288ex; height:10.509ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       where
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle (X_{A}^{0},Y_{A}^{0},Z_{A}^{0})}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <mo stretchy="false">
              (
             </mo>
             <msubsup>
              <mi>
               X
              </mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi>
                A
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mn>
                0
               </mn>
              </mrow>
             </msubsup>
             <mo>
              ,
             </mo>
             <msubsup>
              <mi>
               Y
              </mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi>
                A
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mn>
                0
               </mn>
              </mrow>
             </msubsup>
             <mo>
              ,
             </mo>
             <msubsup>
              <mi>
               Z
              </mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi>
                A
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mn>
                0
               </mn>
              </mrow>
             </msubsup>
             <mo stretchy="false">
              )
             </mo>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle (X_{A}^{0},Y_{A}^{0},Z_{A}^{0})}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="(X_{A}^{0},Y_{A}^{0},Z_{A}^{0})" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fe8f3c6de1f08336d5af9f8198192595e2ac3e8a" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:13.273ex; height:3.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       is the origin for the rotation and scaling transforms and
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <mi mathvariant="normal">
              Δ
              <!-- Δ -->
             </mi>
             <mi>
              S
             </mi>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle \Delta S}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="\Delta S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/15a2efec755f08f95da4e8d1f7f2682861fb59be" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.435ex; height:2.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       is the scaling factor.
      </p>
      <p>
       The Molodensky-Badekas transform is used to transform local geodetic datums to a global geodetic datum, such as WGS 84. Unlike the Helmert transform, the Molodensky-Badekas transform is not reversible due to the rotational origin being associated with the original datum.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OGP7_2_25-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-OGP7_2-25">
         [25]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference nowrap">
        :
        <span>
         134
        </span>
       </sup>
      </p>
